    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer8673488566283429896">“Cut off the head of the snake and another will grow in its place.” <br/> <br/>Part crime drama, part legal thriller, Betrayal in Blue follows the return of Zachary Blake and Jack Dylan as they fight law enforcement itself in picturesque Manistee, Michigan. <br/> <br/>Following its triumph over white supremacists in the field and in the courtroom, law enforcement in the city of Dearborn, Mich</span>
  <span id="freeText8673488566283429896" style="display:none">“Cut off the head of the snake and another will grow in its place.” <br /> <br />Part crime drama, part legal thriller, Betrayal in Blue follows the return of Zachary Blake and Jack Dylan as they fight law enforcement itself in picturesque Manistee, Michigan. <br /> <br />Following its triumph over white supremacists in the field and in the courtroom, law enforcement in the city of Dearborn, Michigan has enjoyed relative tranquility. Unfortunately, not for long, as a second (and more dangerous) syndicate and its leader plot revenge for their fallen brothers. Their scheme? To steal and release deadly Sarin gas in the city. <br /> <br />Police Captain Jack Dylan and his team are dedicated to thwarting the plot and bringing the culprits to justice. However, with a terrorist threat in play, the FBI usurps the investigation. However, Jack Dylan never backs away from a case or a fight. When the white supremacy leader evades the FBI's dragnet, Jack goes rogue and hunts him down in Manistee. <br /> <br />The inevitable standoff finds Dylan alone with his nemesis in an unfamiliar city with no FBI or local law enforcement to support him. His plans go awry, and Jack finds himself arrested by local authorities and placed on trial for his actions. <br /> <br />Attorney Zachary Blake comes to his defense in the biggest trial this quiet community has ever seen. The local cops and the FBI think they have a winner, but Zack and his lead investigator, Micah Love, believe there’s more to the story than meets the eye. <br /> <br />This exciting legal thriller concludes with a dramatic showdown that has become the trademark of award-winning author Mark M. Bello who is, once again, at the top of his game. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8673488566283429896" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

<div id="review_2699907524" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2699907524" />
    <a title="Sherri Moorer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7550002-sherri-moorer"><img alt="Sherri Moorer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558812549p2/7550002.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2699907524?book_show_action=true">Feb 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sherri Moorer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sherri Moorer" href="/user/show/7550002-sherri-moorer">Sherri Moorer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2699907524" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1485289957741133760">Jack Dylan is riding the wake of a triumph over white supremacists in his small town of Dearborn, Michigan, when he discovers that another plot has hatched. The leader of another syndicate has vowed revenge for the arrest of a friend through a sarin attack on Dearborn. Jack and the rest of the Dearborn force are working diligently to thwart the attack when the FBI steps in and ururps the investigation. Frustrated, Jack decides to strike off on his own after the leader when he gets a tip that the</span>
  <span id="freeText1485289957741133760" style="display:none">Jack Dylan is riding the wake of a triumph over white supremacists in his small town of Dearborn, Michigan, when he discovers that another plot has hatched. The leader of another syndicate has vowed revenge for the arrest of a friend through a sarin attack on Dearborn. Jack and the rest of the Dearborn force are working diligently to thwart the attack when the FBI steps in and ururps the investigation. Frustrated, Jack decides to strike off on his own after the leader when he gets a tip that the man behind the sarin plot is on a fishing boat in Manistee. The plot nearly works, until Jack makes a careless mistake that blows his cover, and winds diving in a lake to save himself from a grenade attack. The Manistee police are furious with Jack for launching an undercover operation in their jurisdiction without permission, and arrest him on charges of stalking and suspected murder. Arrested and alone, Jack calls his friend, defense attorney Zachary Blake, to defend him against the charges, clear his name, and unravel the rest of the story that happened on that fishing boat. Betrayal in Blue, by Mark M. Bello, is an entertaining journey through the criminal justice process, from the planned crime to the aftermath of the trial. <br /><br />I like Betrayal in Blue because it shows readers the entire process, from crime to court, and beyond. I learned a great deal about investigations and collecting evidence, and the story is fascinating.Jack Dylan and Zachary Blake may seem stereotypical cops and lawyers on the surface, but this book exposes a deeper character in both of them that shows how their integrity makes them successful. The story is entertaining, and has plenty of twists to keep you wondering how it will end, and even gifts you with a glimpse beyond the end as the story continues past the perceived "ending" of the story. It just goes to show that it's never truly over! I anticipate that Jack and Zachary both have many shared adventures to come. Mark M. Bello has created a compelling world with a rich and diverse cast of characters that make this tale intriguing - and no doubt, will share many more stories to come!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1485289957741133760" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3148331333" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3148331333" />
    <a title="the-librarian" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/103684610-the-librarian"><img alt="the-librarian" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570282445p2/103684610.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3148331333?book_show_action=true">Jan 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="the-librarian" class="user" itemprop="url" name="the-librarian" href="/user/show/103684610-the-librarian">the-librarian</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/49079091-betrayal-in-blue">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3148331333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2428684333537141214">Super lawyer Zachary Blake is back in action in the third installment of the Zachary Blake Legal Thriller series of novels. If you have not read the first two books, you should definitely go out and do so now. Not because it is required to understand this book, but it is a lot of fun to watch the character growth and development from the beginning. If you haven’t read either of them, you can certainly still pick this one up and not be lost though.<br/><br/>This time Zack finds himself fighting against pol</span>
  <span id="freeText2428684333537141214" style="display:none">Super lawyer Zachary Blake is back in action in the third installment of the Zachary Blake Legal Thriller series of novels. If you have not read the first two books, you should definitely go out and do so now. Not because it is required to understand this book, but it is a lot of fun to watch the character growth and development from the beginning. If you haven’t read either of them, you can certainly still pick this one up and not be lost though.<br /><br />This time Zack finds himself fighting against police. FBI resources, and white supremacists (again) to protect his old enemy, Captain Jack Dylan, from false terrorism charges. This time the case takes place in a small northern Michigan fishing town. As with the rest of the series, the book is really well written and is exciting with compelling characters and plenty of plot twists to hold your interest. All of the plot lines hold together and makes for an interesting story overall.<br /><br />Overall, this is another strong entry by author Mark M. Bello. With plenty of interesting investigations, chasing, evidence discovery, and trial intrigue to keep anyones interest for the whole book. If you enjoy a good legal/crime thriller, it would be difficult to go wrong in picking this one up. While you’re at it, you may as well pick up the other two books in the series as well because if you like this one you will definitely want to read the rest of the series.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3478136676" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3478136676" />
    <a title="Bunny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/119369540-bunny"><img alt="Bunny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596527722p2/119369540.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bunny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bunny" href="/user/show/119369540-bunny">Bunny</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3478136676" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18321663393483752240">The third instalment in the Zachary Blake series follows a similar vein as the last book, Betrayal of Justice. This book felt a little more fictional to me while the others seemed very realistic. This doesn't changed the fact that it is still a remarkable book and incredibly well written but in my opinion a little bit more conspiracy based. Regardless, I still throughly enjoyed it and will continue on with this fantastic crime drama series. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2780889949" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2780889949" />
    <a title="Kathleen Kelly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2714432-kathleen-kelly"><img alt="Kathleen Kelly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1308841827p2/2714432.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2780889949?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kathleen Kelly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kathleen Kelly" href="/user/show/2714432-kathleen-kelly">Kathleen Kelly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2780889949" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6534945145793309516">Betrayal in Blue by Mark M. Bello is a story of one man's determination to find the leader of the white supremacists, Bart Breitner. The story starts out with a group of men, the elite unit of the Dearborn Michigan police officers. They received notoriety for arresting a group of white supremacists and in the process exonerating Arya Khan, a Muslim woman who had been accused of killing a mosque bomber, who later was held, hostage. <br/><br/><br/>As this is going on, they find out that there is a plot to releas</span>
  <span id="freeText6534945145793309516" style="display:none">Betrayal in Blue by Mark M. Bello is a story of one man's determination to find the leader of the white supremacists, Bart Breitner. The story starts out with a group of men, the elite unit of the Dearborn Michigan police officers. They received notoriety for arresting a group of white supremacists and in the process exonerating Arya Khan, a Muslim woman who had been accused of killing a mosque bomber, who later was held, hostage. <br /><br /><br />As this is going on, they find out that there is a plot to release a gas called Sarin. This is a gas that was developed by the Germans in 1938, it was used in an attack in Japan, and more recently used in Syria. Now the white supremacists want to use the gas in Washington. The police now need to find out all they can about sarin and the plot. Fortunately, the plot is destroyed and the sarin collected. One of the detectives, Captain Jack Dylan is not happy with all of this, he wants to find Bart Breitner at all costs. Not only that, the Muslim community is endangered and Jack does what he can to notify the community by attending evening worship at Imam Ghafari's Mosque of America to warn the worshipers of their risk from the white supremacists.<br /><br /><br />Jack decides to go after Bart undercover and prepares to go on a fishing trip but wants to go and join Bart's group of supremacists, which he does. Jack does have a group of other police officers as back up for whatever assistance he may need. Unfortunately for Jack, on a meeting on Bart's boat, he accidentally calls Bart Bert which is now a problem for Jack. Bart threatens to shoot Jack. Jack is credulous that Bart would shoot him over a mispronouncing of his name. Now a backup officer listening in, Shaheed, calls 911 for further assistance. Breitner has a grenade and uses it. Jack jumps overboard to protect himself. The local police of Manistee hold Jack and charge him with murder. They sift around for clues and find blood and body parts in the water which is enough for them to arrest him. They don't like that Jack did an undercover investigation on their turf so they don't like Jack and make it as hard for Jack as they can. Jack gets his friend Zack who is a high profile lawyer. Next is a trial and to give away more of the story I will stop here.<br /><br />What I did not like about the book, I couldn't really find anything I did not like about the book, except the bad guys, nothing that the author did or did not do. It was interesting to learn more about sarin and white supremacists. I did not read the previous two books, I would have liked to learn more about the relationship between Jack and his lawyer Zach Blake, so I may just go and read the first two books in the series, as it appears that the author Mark M. Bello knows his stuff when it comes to police procedurals. This book will appeal to the reader who loves the mystery/murder/police procedurals genres there is some violence but not too descriptive. If you don't like this kind of book then I would not recommend it. <br /><br />What I liked about Betrayal in Blue by Mark M. Bello? I am an avid reader of mystery/procedural stories and I really liked this book. It is written professionally, no grammar issues that I could find. The story flowed from beginning to end. The main character, Jack, is a character that you can feel and know that he is a man with issues but has a determination to do the right thing. I was able to read the book without getting bored, a page-turner. This is an intense courtroom drama and I give it 4 out of 4 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6534945145793309516" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

He has battled a corrupt church and white supremacy, but he might be facing his toughest challenge yet when an old foe Police Captain Jack Dylan is accused of murdering a terrorist. It's a race against the clock for Zach and his team investigators and scientists to locate the evidence that will exonerate Jack. Will Zach be able to work his magic in the courtroom for the third time or will Jack los</span>
  <span id="freeText424393356467479631" style="display:none">Redeemed lawyer Zachary Black is back for his third outing, in 'Betrayal in Blue' by Mark M. Bello. He has battled a corrupt church and white supremacy, but he might be facing his toughest challenge yet when an old foe Police Captain Jack Dylan is accused of murdering a terrorist. It's a race against the clock for Zach and his team investigators and scientists to locate the evidence that will exonerate Jack. Will Zach be able to work his magic in the courtroom for the third time or will Jack lose his career, reputation, and freedom?<br /><br />It's another great courtroom thriller from Bello, with plenty of suspense, and again I read most of this book in a single sitting. Like his other novels, Bello creates a charged atmosphere and the plot really keeps you on your toes. I'm already onto book four, and I can't wait to read many more Zach Blake legal thrillers.</span>

The story is very well thought out and feels as realistic as all the other books.   <span id="freeText592515626664790299" style="display:none">This is another great crime thriller from Bello. The plot of this book follows a similar theme as the last regarding a storm brewing in the U.S. around immigration and in particular muslims. The story is very well thought out and feels as realistic as all the other books. The plot is riveting and the the switching between characters (in all of the books I've read so far) is a great way to see all points of view regardless of whether you agree with them or not, and that's even more important when the events feel so realistic. I'm really enjoying the series and can't wait to get to the next one. </span>

<div id="review_2469619443" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2469619443" />
    <a title="Samyuktha Ell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23965736-samyuktha-ell"><img alt="Samyuktha Ell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1581762910p2/23965736.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2469619443?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samyuktha Ell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samyuktha Ell" href="/user/show/23965736-samyuktha-ell">Samyuktha Ell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2469619443" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3790849341709269611">Betrayal in Blue is a fictional thriller written by Mark M. Bello. It begins by introducing us to the Dearborn Police Department (PD) that has just managed to retrieve a piece of information on the dark web about the possible plotting of a terror mission directed at Dearborn, its cops, and Muslims. <br/><br/>Jack Dylan is a veteran of the Dearborn PD, and his team’s key members include Andy Toller―forensic criminologist, Noah Thompson―cybercrime expert, and Shaheed Ali―Muslim affairs expert. The team is m</span>
  <span id="freeText3790849341709269611" style="display:none">Betrayal in Blue is a fictional thriller written by Mark M. Bello. It begins by introducing us to the Dearborn Police Department (PD) that has just managed to retrieve a piece of information on the dark web about the possible plotting of a terror mission directed at Dearborn, its cops, and Muslims. <br /><br />Jack Dylan is a veteran of the Dearborn PD, and his team’s key members include Andy Toller―forensic criminologist, Noah Thompson―cybercrime expert, and Shaheed Ali―Muslim affairs expert. The team is more like a friendship forged over many years.<br /><br />Since I hadn’t read the last two instalments in the series, it took me a while to get into this story. For the first few chapters, you are introduced to a number of different characters who seem to have mostly been part of the previous books in the series. <br /><br />The story takes place in a time where racism is still quite alive and violence and attacks against minorities are a prominent feature of the society. There is also a lot of legal drama in the story, which―to me―was the highlight of the book. <br /></span>

<div id="review_3434088314" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3434088314" />
    <a title="Pegboard" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard"><img alt="Pegboard" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498516338p2/47722544.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3434088314?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pegboard" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pegboard" href="/user/show/47722544-pegboard">Pegboard</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3434088314" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3541464436939811787">Betrayal in Blue is Mark M. Bello’s third novel in A Zachary Blake Legal Thriller, and I think it is the best so far. Police Captain Jack Dylan is in hot pursuit of a white supremacist, Bart Breitner, who is seeking revenge for capturing his leader. After the FBI messed up the only lead they had, Jack goes after him undercover, as a civilian. When Jack gets himself in trouble, he calls Zack Blake. Can Zack pull the evidence together in time to clear Jack’s name?<br/> <br/>I love Mark M. Bello’s Zachary Bl</span>
  <span id="freeText3541464436939811787" style="display:none">Betrayal in Blue is Mark M. Bello’s third novel in A Zachary Blake Legal Thriller, and I think it is the best so far. Police Captain Jack Dylan is in hot pursuit of a white supremacist, Bart Breitner, who is seeking revenge for capturing his leader. After the FBI messed up the only lead they had, Jack goes after him undercover, as a civilian. When Jack gets himself in trouble, he calls Zack Blake. Can Zack pull the evidence together in time to clear Jack’s name?<br /> <br />I love Mark M. Bello’s Zachary Blake legal thrillers. As with each book, Betrayal in Blue can be read by itself, but you get the picture of the characters if you read them in order. Zachary Blake is a dedicated and thorough attorney, who will employ all his resources to clear his clients. The author implements a complex web of mystery and drama that will keep the reader glued to the pages. Overall, I loved reading this novel and look forward to Betrayal in Black.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3541464436939811787" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review3434088314">

<div id="review_3440850108" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3440850108" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3440850108?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/49079091-betrayal-in-blue">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3440850108" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16715158267407280671">From initial investigation to the ultimate trial – another incendiary adventure!<br/><br/>Michigan author Mark M. Bello is an attorney and a justice advocate, having earned his BA in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree form Thomas M. Cooley Law School. He spent forty years in the courtroom with high profile legal cases, and now offers his knowledge on his website Legal Examiner and Injury Board writing posts about safety, fairness and justice in the civil justice system. Mark con</span>
  <span id="freeText16715158267407280671" style="display:none">From initial investigation to the ultimate trial – another incendiary adventure!<br /><br />Michigan author Mark M. Bello is an attorney and a justice advocate, having earned his BA in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree form Thomas M. Cooley Law School. He spent forty years in the courtroom with high profile legal cases, and now offers his knowledge on his website Legal Examiner and Injury Board writing posts about safety, fairness and justice in the civil justice system. Mark consolidates his experiences in this series of novels – THE ZACHARY BLAKE LEGAL THRILLERS, of which BETRAYAL IN BLUE is Book 3.<br /><br />One reason Mark M Bello’s legal thriller series is so absorbing is the manner in which he draws parallels to contemporary controversies. In this series Bello has tackled the Church and clergy sexual abuse, white supremacists and the President of the US, and now law enforcement. Though this book was written in 2019, it is uncanny how prescient are the author’s observations in novel format – ideas that are currently consuming the media and our minds and lives at this moment in time. <br /><br />By now, those who follow the Zachary Blake legal thrillers know the primary characters and the unique mode of communicating a story line that make these books so memorable: the need for introductions is less important, but Bello adds new personnel in this volume and in doing so stirs even more reflective thoughts! <br /><br />The synopsis is a fine guide for this fast paced story – ‘White Supremacy again rears its ugly head in Dearborn. Trial lawyer Zachary Blake returns along with Dearborn Police Captain Jack Dylan for an exciting journey through investigation, chase, deception, forensics, and trial. Jack is in trouble with the law in a quaint northern Michigan fishing town, accused of murdering a terrorist. The local police and the FBI join forces to take him down. To prove his innocence—Captain Jack turns to an old nemesis . . . Zachary Blake. A dynamic cast of characters converges on Manistee, Michigan for the biggest trial this small fishing town has ever seen. Can Zack and Jack prevent the brotherhood in blue from morphing into a Betrayal in Blue?’ And once again the story rings true, especially in view of contemporary news.<br /><br />After reading the first two volumes, the central character Zachary Blake is now a substantial legal hero, and the manner in which master craftsman Bello manipulates his character’s movement and development is a witness to both the depth of his legal knowledge and his eloquent prose. The language is appropriate for each character, and the manner in which the multiple characters interweave is mesmerizing. This legal thriller series is of the first caliber! Highly recommended. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16715158267407280671" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText3277972616664033492" style="display:none">This third book in the Zachary Blake Legal Thriller Series by Mark M Bello was definitely a fast-paced thrill ride combining action involving an unofficial police battle with a White Supremacist along with a tense legal battle in court defending that police officer. Zack utilizes his usual group of experts to hopefully find that one key piece of evidence that will or will not exonerate his client. The characters in this book are fairly well described and fleshed out. The story moves along a nice even pace from opening salvo to the final words. I am looking forward to reading book 4 in this series which I already have in my TBR file. This is a voluntary review of this book from Fast and Free Reviews.</span>

Noah Thompson handed Captain Jack Dylan a website message: Sarin in Dearborn. <br />Shaheed Ali (Jack’s right-hand man) explained to them what sarin gas does to a human. <br />The Free America Party (white supremacist/nationalist organization in<br />Lexington, KT. Barton “Bart” Breitner (bigot/anti-Semite) was the group’s leader. <br />Asher “Ash” Granger former Officer, who was fired, betrayed Benjamin Blaine (85, The Conservative Council head). So, Benjamin killed him.<br /><br />Jefferson Marina. Sinbad’s Restaurant. Jillian’s Dream (sailboat). Captain Dylan &amp; ADA Wolfe came aboard. <br />Jonathan “Jon” Stone (The Free America Party member, Eastpointe, MI) introduced himself to the 2 of them.<br />Shirley’s Bar &amp; Grill. White Knight (46’ Trojan fishing boat) Jack Manning &amp; Captain Dylan were not going to let Barton “Bart” Breitner (airport air traffic controller) get the best of him. <br />BOOM!<br /><br />Captain Dylan is going to be charged for 1st degree murder of Barton “Bart” Breitner. <br />Zack called Micah Love (husband/father, Love investigations).<br />Zachary “Zack” Blake (Jack’s attorney), Micah &amp; Matt Jordan (Micah’s CSI) were meeting with Chief Alexander.<br />Manistee, MI. 85th District Court (3rd St.). All rise. District Court for the County of Manistee is now in session. The Honorable District Court Judge Joseph Abernathy is presiding. <br />State v. Dylan. <br />DA Jarrod Weaver (Manistee County) Zachary Blake (defense attorney) <br />Jack Dylan (defendant) is charged with 1st degree murder of Barton Breitner (FBI terrorist watch list). <br />Not-guilty plea your Honor. <br />Bail is set at $500,000 cash or bond.<br />3 hrs. later, Jack’s bond was raised/posted.<br /><br />The trial continued. <br />Manistee, MI. 85th District Court (3rd St.). All rise. District Court for the County of Manistee is now in session. The Honorable District Court Judge Paul E. Shipley is presiding. <br />State v. Dylan. <br />How will Jack’s trial turn out? <br /><br />The only thing I found wrong with this book is the split screen format. I don’t like reading this type! <br /><br />I do not receive any type of compensation for reading &amp; reviewing free books from publishers &amp; authors. Therefore, I am under no obligation to write a positive review, only an honest one. <br /><br />Warning: This book contains descriptive accounts of extremely graphic adult content, violence (terrorism), or expletive language &amp;/or uncensored sexually explicit material which is only suitable for mature readers. It may be offensive or have potential adverse psychological effects on the reader. If you are especially sensitive to this type of material, it is strongly advised not to read any further.<br /><br />An awesome book cover, great font &amp; writing style. A very professionally written terrorist thriller book. It was extremely easy for me to read/follow from start/finish &amp; never a dull moment. There were no grammar/typo errors, nor any repetitive or out of line sequence sentences. Lots of exciting scenarios, with several twists/turns &amp; a great description list of unique characters, settings, facts etc. to keep track of. This could also make another great terrorist thriller movie, or better yet a mini TV series. To be continued. An amazingly easy rating of 5 stars. <br /><br />Thank you for the free author; 8 Grand Publications; Goodreads; MakingConnections; Making Connections discussion group talk; ARR Amazon createspace; PDF book. <br />Tony Parsons MSW (Washburn)<br /></span>

  <span id="freeText255432917207582529" style="display:none">This is the 4th book of the series that I have read. Even though I was aware of the final conclusion, I was still interested to read this and found out all of the details.<br /><br />This story has the Dearborn Police task force discovering a plot against them as well as a Muslim mosque in their town because of their success in bring another White Supremacist group to justice earlier and this new group wanted revenge. The information eventually gets provided to the FBI who immediately takes control of the case. While an operation was set up by the FBI to thwart the White Supremacist group from obtaining chemical weapons. They were successful except for the fact that the leader of this group escaped.<br /><br />Jack Daly the Captain on the Task Force received information that he used to go undercover to capture this individual. Unfortunately, all did not go like planned and Jack was charged with murder of the group leader. Zach was hired to defend Jack and with the assistance of Micah Love's team and 3 of the task force members, they were able to obtain evidence which could aide Zach with Jack's defense.<br /><br />The description of how the evidence was gathered and the actual trail really plays into the meat of the book. The ending is well worth it and has a surprise in it. To find out how the whole story ends, then you must read this book. You won't be disappointed.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amie" href="/user/show/41406182-amie">Amie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2806644752" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6093359804805542461"><strong>Fast paced crime novel</strong><br/><br/>Betrayal in Blue is a fast pace crime novel, the 3rd in the Zackary Blake series.  This series follows Dearborn, IL police captain Jack Dylan’s hunt for justice and Attorney Zachary Blake’s struggle to ensure that justice is enforced.  In this latest novel, Betrayal in Blue, Jack finds himself once again up against White Supremacist Terrorists as his team uncovers a plot to release a deadly attack on a Mosque in Dearborn.  Jack and his team strive to glean as much intel as </span>
  <span id="freeText6093359804805542461" style="display:none"><strong>Fast paced crime novel</strong><br /><br />Betrayal in Blue is a fast pace crime novel, the 3rd in the Zackary Blake series.  This series follows Dearborn, IL police captain Jack Dylan’s hunt for justice and Attorney Zachary Blake’s struggle to ensure that justice is enforced.  In this latest novel, Betrayal in Blue, Jack finds himself once again up against White Supremacist Terrorists as his team uncovers a plot to release a deadly attack on a Mosque in Dearborn.  Jack and his team strive to glean as much intel as they can before alerting the boys in the FBI and risking a hostile takeover of their investigation. Much to Jack’s unhappiness the FBI are soon on top of Jack’s team and when things go array during a take down of the supremacist group, the main player escapes into thin air. Jack takes it upon himself to right the wrong and searches out  the leader on his own. <br />Jack quickly finds the suspect and then finds himself accused of murder.   Indicted by a small town police chief, hell bent on making an example of Jack for his big  city bravado and lack of professional courtesy; things don’t look good for Jack. <br />Luckily Jack has distinguished defense attorney Zachary Blake in his back pocket. Will Blake be able to not just acquit his client of all charges but prove him innocent and save his career as a decorated law officer?<br /> Betray in Blue is an action packed novel full of suspense and unexpected twists.  Written like a true crime novel Betrayal in Blue has you feeling like you are part of the investigation team, privy to all the discoveries as they unfold. Well written, well plotted and leaving you loving the main players more and more, Betray in Blue earns a solid 4 stars.  <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17592871972398358218">Betrayal in Blue is a very well written legal thriller set in the cities of Dearborn and Manistee, Michigan. The city of Dearborn has recently recovered from the bombing of a Muslim mosque and the ensuing trial of  Arya Khan, a Muslim woman accused of setting the bomb. Attorney Zachary Blake represents Arya and she is found innocent. The true culprits were a group of white supremacists. When their leader is arrested and found guilty of the crime, his followers plan to seek revenge with yet anoth</span>
  <span id="freeText17592871972398358218" style="display:none">Betrayal in Blue is a very well written legal thriller set in the cities of Dearborn and Manistee, Michigan. The city of Dearborn has recently recovered from the bombing of a Muslim mosque and the ensuing trial of  Arya Khan, a Muslim woman accused of setting the bomb. Attorney Zachary Blake represents Arya and she is found innocent. The true culprits were a group of white supremacists. When their leader is arrested and found guilty of the crime, his followers plan to seek revenge with yet another terrorist act in Dearborn. When Captain Jack Dylan, head of the city’s Terrorism Task Force is notified about the possibility that the city is again being targeted, he and his team are determined to make sure any act of terrorism doesn’t happen, but the FBI steps in to derail their plans. One very dangerous man escapes under the FBI’s watch and an angry Jack Dylan decides to go after him on his own.<br /><br /><br />In his haste to find and arrest the terrorist, Captain Dylan heads to Manistee and goes undercover without notice to any of the authorities in Dearborn, Manistee or to the FBI. When his plans begin to go terribly wrong he finds himself arrested by the local authorities for his deceptive actions.<br /><br /><br />In deep trouble and in need of representation, attorney Zachary Blake shows up on the scene to defend Jack. It’s a royal battle for Zachary when all evidence points to his client’s guilt. With Zachary being one of the best attorneys in MIchigan and a team of experts on hand he goes all out to win and find a smoking gun that could help find Jack innocent.<br /><br /><br />This a mind-blowing story with a shocking and intense ending that will have readers sitting on the edge of their seats.</span>

<div id="review_2686746665" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2686746665" />
    <a title="Terra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32592656-terra"><img alt="Terra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505592270p2/32592656.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2686746665?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Terra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Terra" href="/user/show/32592656-terra">Terra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2686746665" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15888499493338972247"><br/>Betrayal in Blue was written by Mark M. Bello and recently released on Sept 21, 2018. It is the third book in a series about Jack Dylan a captain in the Dearborn, Michigan police department. He continues his fight with a new white supremacist group bent on exacting revenge of Benjamin Blaine’s (A white supremacist leader from the earlier book Betrayal of Justice) capture. The Free America Party wants to use sarin gas to attack a Muslim church in Dearborn and take down the Dearborn police departm</span>
  <span id="freeText15888499493338972247" style="display:none"><br />Betrayal in Blue was written by Mark M. Bello and recently released on Sept 21, 2018. It is the third book in a series about Jack Dylan a captain in the Dearborn, Michigan police department. He continues his fight with a new white supremacist group bent on exacting revenge of Benjamin Blaine’s (A white supremacist leader from the earlier book Betrayal of Justice) capture. The Free America Party wants to use sarin gas to attack a Muslim church in Dearborn and take down the Dearborn police department. From there the unexpected begins! I have rated this book two out of four stars. I really loved the surprise elements in the book, the plot points and the in-depth knowledge of weapons and courtroom proceedings while I struggled with the character building, descriptions of settings and the motives of certain characters which impacted my overall rating of the book.<br /><br />I truly enjoy my crime dramas which made this book an easy read. It moved along at a good pace. Just when I was ready for the next plot point in the book it delivered. I loved not knowing what to expect, while being surprised and wondering how these new developments will change my expectations of the ending of the story. My favorite part in the book is when Jack Dylan on his own time goes after Bart Breitner the leader of the Free America Party to the small town of Manistee, Michigan. Next thing you know instead of arresting Bart Breitner... I can’t tell tell you because it would be a spoiler.<br /><br />Bello clearly has done his research into the technical parts of the story. It was obvious he had in-depth knowledge about sarin gas, weapons, tactical police teams. Bello was a lawyer before he became an author and it really showed in Zachary Blake’s character as the defense attorney for Jack Dylan. In fact Zachary Blake ended up being my favorite character because it was clear Bello loved to write about him. Zack was smart, thoughtful, witty and clearly was a great attorney. <br /><br />While all these parts were fun and enjoyable, I really struggled with the character building, descriptions of people and settings. There was a lot of telling and not showing in this book such as I never really knew what Jack Dylan looks like other than “distinguished looking middle-aged man who was graying at the temples.” pg. 7 What is his ethnicity? How tall is he? What is the color of his eyes? I also don’t know anything about Jack. Was he born in Dearborn Michigan? Why did he become a cop? Does he have any family? Was he married? Does he have any kids? Why did he defy explicit orders to track down Breitner knowing he could lose his career over it? There wasn’t enough description or background to really show why someone as smart as Jack decided it was worth it to risk it all.<br /><br />I really wanted to give this book three out of four stars but I couldn’t. There were too many holes and gaps in the story. When Jack get bailed out of jail in one scene where does he stay? What is he thinking? A man of action won’t be happy with staying cooped up but there was nothing written at all while his lawyer was building his defense. Also, Bart Bretiner doesn’t seem to have any motive to being a white supremacist. The level of planning Bart Bretiner went to bomb the Muslim church he couldn’t have just been an average racist.There was no background on his life that led him on this path. It made his character unbelievable.<br /><br />The character building and descriptions are what really makes me fall in love with stories. I need texture, color, layers. I want the towns that Jack was in to have their own personality. I wanted to see the kind of culture and society of the people they held within their walls. It helps give motives to the people in the story. It makes the characters more alive. I didn’t find it in this book at all and I think it is why I struggled with the linchpin of the story, which I can’t tell you about because I don’t want to give any spoilers.<br /><br />Overall, I had to rate this book two out of four stars for these reasons. It doesn’t mean I didn’t like the story. If a reader is looking for a book that is all about action, then I recommend it! It is perfect for reading while stuck in a layover at an airport or a fun summer camping read or snuggled up on the couch during a rainy day.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15888499493338972247" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2700787853?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bonnie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bonnie" href="/user/show/44364621-bonnie">Bonnie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2700787853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12059049273908138540">Three Stars for Betrayal in Blue by Mark M. Bello. This is the third book in this series, but the first one I have read. References were made to the subject of the first book, but if you didn’t read it, it doesn’t impact the gist of the third. If references were made from the second book, I did not notice them.<br/><br/>Mr. Bello tells a great story. It was engaging throughout, and the entire time reading it, I thought it would make a good movie or TV show. The main character, Jack Dylan, is an honorable </span>
  <span id="freeText12059049273908138540" style="display:none">Three Stars for Betrayal in Blue by Mark M. Bello. This is the third book in this series, but the first one I have read. References were made to the subject of the first book, but if you didn’t read it, it doesn’t impact the gist of the third. If references were made from the second book, I did not notice them.<br /><br />Mr. Bello tells a great story. It was engaging throughout, and the entire time reading it, I thought it would make a good movie or TV show. The main character, Jack Dylan, is an honorable police officer, and it’s clear he has a cohesive team. <br /><br />Dylan tells his boss he needs some R and R, then goes out of town to chase after a terrorist by himself. Only a few select people know what he’s up to. This is when things backfire on him and is is arrested for murder. The local police force and FBI think he’s guilty rather than backing him up, despite the lack of evidence and lack of a dead body.<br /><br />The chapters involving the trial were the best. It was like being there. I loved Judge Shipley’s personality and reasonableness. Zack, Jack’s defense attorney, is likeable as well. You have to feel for the prosecutor somewhat, and Chief Alexander? He’s the guy you love to hate.<br /><br />The story itself is a good 3 stars and has potential for 4 stars, except I found the dialogue did not flow as well as it could have. In many places it seemed too formal and unnatural somehow, however, the courtroom dialogue was stellar. <br /><br />I read this book on kindle, and perhaps that is the reason why there are formatting issues. There were paragraphs highlighted, but there was nothing special in the highlighted areas to suggest the highlighting was intentional. There were several paragraphs needing indentation, a handful of punctuation mishaps, and sentences that read awkwardly or the editing was not proofread. The number of semicolons used throughout the book was a bit distracting. <br /><br />I would definitely read more from this author, but hope the next book I read from him is edited better.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12059049273908138540" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2978210058" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

        <a title="Mehrnaz Siavoshi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mehrnaz Siavoshi" href="/user/show/32030371-mehrnaz-siavoshi">Mehrnaz Siavoshi</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2978210058" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8333663065094095800"><a href='https://forums.onlinebookclub.org/viewtopic.php?f=22&t=120477' rel='nofollow noopener'>Full review and discussion here. </a><br/><br/><i>I received a free copy of this book in exchange for an honest review.</i><br/><br/>This was a super fast-paced book that I was able to get through surprisingly quickly. It tells the story of Dearborn Police Captain Jack Dylan’s struggles to capture white supremacist and terrorist Barton Breitner. The story as a whole was exciting, but it was highly predictable and followed every trope I could think of in the legal thriller genre. Overall, I give it <b>
  <u>3.25 stars</u>
</b>. <br/><br/>The highligh</span>
  <span id="freeText8333663065094095800" style="display:none"><a href="https://forums.onlinebookclub.org/viewtopic.php?f=22&amp;t=120477" rel="nofollow noopener">Full review and discussion here. </a><br /><br /><i>I received a free copy of this book in exchange for an honest review.</i><br /><br />This was a super fast-paced book that I was able to get through surprisingly quickly. It tells the story of Dearborn Police Captain Jack Dylan’s struggles to capture white supremacist and terrorist Barton Breitner. The story as a whole was exciting, but it was highly predictable and followed every trope I could think of in the legal thriller genre. Overall, I give it <b>
  <u>3.25 stars</u>
</b>. <br /><br />The highlights of this book are its fast pace. There was no point in reading it where I was bored, even though it does follow a predictable structure. While the structure itself was predictable and I knew a plot twist was coming, the specific plot twists were interesting and thought out. <br /><br />The one biggest thing that took me out of the book was the research-based parts. There was a section in particular where one character was explaining what sarin gas was to another and I felt like that section could have come straight out of a Wikipedia article.<br /><br />Ultimately, I don't think this book is bad. I think it deserves a lot of the same criticisms that crime dramas like Law and Order: SVU get, but that does not make it a poor book. In fact, I would recommend this book wholeheartedly to anyone who loves those types of shows. <br /><br />It didn't do anything exciting or change the genre for me. In fact, I would not say this book is memorable. All this together is why I rated it at 3.25 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8333663065094095800" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked

    }
  }

    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

She sees them—literally, and had been seeing the dead ever since she can remember. She tried telling her parents about it when she was a child, but they’d vehemently dismissed it to imaginary friends, so she’d stopped talking about it. There were only two people who actually knew Nonie’s secret and knew she was the real deal. One was Buggy Mouton, her best friend since kindergarten, and the other was Guy Skinard, whom Nonie considered her one true love since the day she’d laid eyes on him in high school. Buggy now worked at MeeMaw’s Café off of Main in Clay Point, and Guy, as usual, remained ever at her side—the only difference being he’d died in a freak boating accident nine years ago. Still the prankster even in death, Guy loved causing chaos, especially with men Nonie occasionally dated. She could only imagine what mayhem he might stir up while mirroring her at the funeral home and mingling with the newly departed.Only hours into the first day of her new job, pandemonium engulfs the funeral home, and much to Nonie’s surprise, it has nothing to do with Guy. It’s brought on by the family they’re serving. Seventy-two–year-old Dover Fontenot, the Major of Clay Point, dies in a car accident after indulging in a little extra-curricular activity—only the activity wasn’t with his wife , Hazel. And when Dover’s mistress, Anna Mae Turner, shows up at the funeral home for the visitation hell’s gates rip open and Broussard’s Funeral Home suddenly turns into a geriatric war zone.Amidst the flying hairpieces, canes and curses, Nonie’s best friend, Buggy, decides to drop by the funeral home with news she can’t wait to share. A cable network in New Orleans wants to put together a paranormal investigation team and have them check out purported haunted locations in Louisiana. For every location with solid filming potential, each member of the team gets a five hundred dollar pay check. And Buggy knows without question that if anyone can sniff out the ‘restless’ dead, it’s Nonie.Knowing nothing about paranormal investigation, but lured by the sound of the adventure and the dollar signs circling through her head, Nonie agrees to become part of the Boo Krewe, the name Buggy has formally given the makeshift team.The lure of money may be one thing, but what Nonie doesn’t realize is that occasionally the dead, so excited that someone can actually see and hear them, decide to follow her home, into her bed—the bathroom—the shower. And adding to this new-found frustration, Nonie barely finishes her first investigation when she gets a visit from Anna Mae Turner—the mayor’s former mistress—now dead, as well, and harassingly Above al<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText10573289564351342027\" style=\"display:none\">From the Foreword by Marian Wright EdelmanAfrica’s Child is an unforgettable and searingly personal book….In the face of repeated obstacles and injustices, Nhambu continued to analyze the world around her with wit and a sharp sense of humor. Above all, as a very young child she decided one day that even if there was no other person in the world who loved and wanted her, she was going to love and care for herself—and that decision changed the course of her life. Africa’s Child is the story of a mixed-race girl growing up in the Usambara Mountains of Tanzania, East Africa. Raised in an orphanage with no knowledge of her origins or family, she endured abandonment, hardships, severe illnesses, and bullying. Her experiences as a child and teenager included physical, emotional, and sexual abuse, social stigma, and racial discrimination.Yet Nhambu tells her inspiring story with warmth and humor. Her questioning mind probes the African tribal realities and multi-cultural complexities that impacted her life both at the orphanage and schools run by German nuns as well as at an African high school with American nuns. Nhambu not only survived her childhood but triumphed. Her faith and resilience, along with a belief in learning and her tenacious pursuit of an education, sustained her through many challenges. Dance, especially African tribal dance, became the way she healed and nourished her spirit. Through the love and commitment of an American teacher she met in Africa, Nhambu was able to pursue her dream of education and a new life for herself. The first book in her three-part memoir ends as she is leaving Africa for university studies in America on a full scholarship.Maria Nhambu is the creator of Aerobics With Soul®, a fitness workout based on African dance. <\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"10573289564351342027\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n    <\/div>\n\n      <div <span id="freeTextContainer11517456542141699601">Mark M. Bello is an attorney, lawsuit finance expert, and award-winning author. A Michigan native, Mark received his B.A. in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree from Thomas M.   <span id="freeText11517456542141699601" style="display:none">Mark M. Bello is an attorney, lawsuit finance expert, and award-winning author. A Michigan native, Mark received his B.A. in English Literature from Oakland University and his law degree from Thomas M. Cooley Law School.<br /><br />After years of working high profile legal cases, Mark wanted to provide a front row glimpse of what a victim faces when standing up for justice. Each book in the Zachary Blake Betrayal Series is a ripped from the headlines novel inspired by not only Bello’s legal experiences, but his concern for our current sociopolitical landscape. With a creative writing style, he tackles themes of religious freedom, racial and ethnic prejudice, human rights, government influence, and law enforcement.<br /><br />Mark is married and has four adult children and eight grandchildren. In addition to his novels, Mark writes articles/blogs about safety, justice, and fairness in the legal system. His work can be found in numerous print and online publications.<br /><br />Mark is currently working on his fourth novel, set for release in 2019.<br />.<br /><br /> <br /><br />**Visit and follow Mark’s blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.markmbello.com">www.markmbello.com</a><br />**Follow Mark on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/MarkMBelloBooks">www.facebook.com/MarkMBelloBooks</a><br />**Follow Mark on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/MarkMBelloBooks">www.twitter.com/MarkMBelloBooks</a><br />** Follow Mark on Goodreads: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/16283795.Mark_M_Bello">www.goodreads.com/author/show/1628379...</a><br /></span>

However, through an unfortunate series of events, Zachary has gone from the penthouse to the poorhouse, working out of a dingy one-room office, handling traffic cases. Although Jennifer has misgivings, she reluctantly retains him and, together, they embark on a &quot;David vs. Goliath&quot; legal battle against an organization hell-bent on thwarting their efforts. Zachary hires an investigator, the infamous Micah Love, who travels to Ohio, where he discovers that two families have disappeared after an encounter with the same priest-and the one person who may provide some answers has died under mysterious circumstances. Religion, law, betrayal, mystery, intrigue, faith, and love converge in Michigan for the trial of the century. Will Zachary resurrect his troubled career and obtain the justice Jennifer seeks for her kids? This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
